I booked a lake view room. The room was a bit small and had a strange smell, but it was quite clean. However, the stains on the cushions on the sofa were very obvious.

The swimming pool is on the fifth floor. Go in through the gym. You can enter the locker room by swiping your card at the front desk. You can go through the locker room and go up the stairs.

It is indeed very popular on the Internet. There are also foreigners checking in and taking pictures. The water quality is also good. The lifeguard said that new water is added every day. If you go swimming in the afternoon, you will not be exposed to the sun at 9 or 10 in the morning.

The most unbearable thing is that the lights in the bathroom cannot be turned on and off independently. They can only be turned on or off. The smart toilet is very loud and the pillows are uncomfortable.

The breakfast on the second day was comparable to more than 100 chain hotels outside, and there was basically nothing to eat.

The most outrageous thing was check-out. When we checked in, we were given a small card with a lot of notes. We knew that if we checked out after 12 o'clock, we would be charged an extra half day's room fee, so we went back to the room after 11 o'clock to take a shower and pack our things, and called the front desk at 11:30. Came here to remind us to check out at 12 o'clock. Within 10 minutes, a staff member knocked on the door to ask if we wanted to extend our stay. Was he worried that we would not leave without paying? Super bad feeling

I feel that this hotel is not a luxury hotel. The price is luxurious but the facilities and services are not up to par.

This means that if I can't live, I have to pay the money, and there is no refund! 3. After paying a deposit of 500 yuan, 300 yuan will be directly deducted when checking out the next day, and only 200 yuan will be refunded. 4. I have stayed in at least hundreds of hotels at home and abroad, and I have never encountered such a thing. Although there is not much money, it is very frustrating!
